2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey Checklist Guide

Checklist Insider EditorDec 5, 2025Dec 5, 2025
  1. Home
  2. Hockey Cards
  3. 2024-25 Hockey Cards
  4. 2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey Checklist Guide

Release Date: December 3, 2025

Brands

Clicking any links and making a purchase can result in this site earning a commission, including the eBay Partner Network and others.

Arriving a few months into the '25-26 season, 2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey is late, as usual, but UD hopes the wait is worth it for fans of the high-end NHL card brand.

Every Hobby box tin averages one Base Rookie Autographed Patch, one serial-numbered autograph relic, booklet or printing plate, and one additional autograph.

  • Review other 2024-25 Hockey Card Guides.
  • 2023-24 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey Checklist Guide.
  • 2022-23 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey Checklist Guide.

2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey Checklist Rundown

Offering some of the most popular high-end rookie cards of the season, the 2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey checklist highlights the 2024 rookie class across multiple lines, with many adding on-card signatures. Collectors can also count on plenty of current and retired stars.

Among the many chases, one special Hot Box contains only Macklin Celebrini cards.

Base & Insert Details

Up first for 2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey, the Base Set is limited to 249 copies, and every box has two cards from this selection.

Among the inserts, Elegant Etchings (/199) is a new choice that promises unique cardstock.

There are also Rookie Masterpiece Press Plates (1/1) and 2024-25 Upper Deck Printing Plate Booklets (1/1).

Autographs Details

Signed cards are again a huge part of The Cup, including Base Gold Spectrum Foil Variation Auto (/12) and Base Rookie Auto Gold Spectrum Foil Variation (/36 or less), plus parallels.

That's just the start of the autographed content in 2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey.

Elegant Etchings and Lavish provide new looks to check out.

Color Coded (/35) pairs team colors and a white ink signature.

UD classics are also back, like Enshrinements (#'d) and more.

Autograph Relic Details

There are even more autographed relics in the 2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey checklist.

This starts in the Base Rookie Auto Patch series (/249 or 99), with every box having one RPA from this subset. These cards again come slabbed and authenticated by Authority.

The Base Rookie Auto Shield Black Foil (1/1) parallel is one of the key chases in the product.

Materialisticks Auto (/15) combines a jersey swatch, a stick relic and a signature.

In addition, the many book cards are sure to receive extra attention, such as the Autographed Monumental Patch Booklets (1/1) set.

The new Autographed Monumental Puck Booklet (1/1) cards boast game-used puck relics and on-card signatures.

Of course, there's much more to discover in The Cup.

Relic Details

That brings us to the unsigned relics in 2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey. Joining the Base Relics (/8 or less) are many more memorabilia choices.

Displaying quality relic swatches, the Patron Patches (#'d) cards appear for the first time.

There are also multi-piece editions, like the Cup Foundations Quad Jersey cards for veterans and rookies.

2024-25 Exquisite Collection / 2024-25 UD Splendor Details

Although The Cup has enough firepower on its own, there are some bonus brands to uncover in 2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey.

Exquisite Collection makes its mark with Exquisite Collection Black (/99) inserts and more.

Young talent is found in Exquisite Collection Rookie Auto Patch (#'d), with jersey-numbered rarity.

There's also a shoutout to the past, thanks to 2003-04 Exquisite Autograph Patch Black. These rare cards put a dark finish on the classic NBA design first released over two decades ago.

UD Splendor is another option with limited Splendor Auto Patch (/36), Splendor Rookie Auto Patch (/36) and Splendor Patch (/36) cards.

Estimated Release Date: December 3, 2025

2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey Product Configuration

Hobby Boxes

  • 6 cards per pack; 1 pack per tin box; 6 tin boxes per case

2024-25 Upper Deck The Cup Hockey Box Break

Hobby Boxes (on average)

  • 1 Base Rookie Autographed Patch
  • 1 Autograph, Autograph Jersey OR Autograph Booklet
  • 1 #'d Autograph Relic, Booklet OR Printing Plate
  • 1 Base Card (/249)
  • 2 Additional Cards (Base, Insert, Relic, Printing Plate AND/OR Redemption)
